URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS100157343	2013-04-09 00:18:10	33080	spuh	warbler sp. (Parulidae sp.)	Parulidae sp.			1				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Lincoln	US-NV-017	US-NV_976	9	USFWS_534		Pahranagat NWR--Middle Marsh	L226215	H	37.2489485	-115.1106262	2010-10-17		obsr209998	S7015166	Incidental	P20	EBIRD				1	0		0	1	0			In Middle Marsh I found a large flock of warblers in the trees between the road through Middle Marsh and HWY 93.  I immediately keyed in on a bird that appeared to be a Blackburnian Warbler.  But I got to looking at it closer and began to realize it was not a Blackburnian as it did not have pale braces on the upper back or a yellowish forehead mark.  And in fact the face pattern wasnt right either.  What the heck was this thing?  I stayed with it photographing it and trying to figure out what I was looking at.  I managed to get quite a few photos but with my cameras focusing problem and the poor lighting conditions, none of the photos are real sharp.  But they still show all the interesting features of this bird.  By studying the combination of features my best guess is a hybrid Townsends x Black-throated Gray Warbler.  Although of course I am just speculating and I dont know if this combination has even ever been recorded before.
